    @pytest.mark.error
    def test_duplicate_force_disabled_400(
        self,
        service_factory,
        local_source_server,
    ) -> None:
        """Duplicate `force` parameters return HTTP 400 with cache disabled."""
        path = "/duplicate_force_disabled.csv"
